</div></span></div>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Personality">Personality</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FAshura_Doji%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D3&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 180px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/0/0a/Ashura_Studying.png/revision/latest?cb=20210214043904" class="image"><img alt="Ashura Studying" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="180" height="111" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Ashura Studying.png" data-image-key="Ashura_Studying.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/0/0a/Ashura_Studying.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20210214043904" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/0/0a/Ashura_Studying.png/revision/latest?cb=20210214043904" class="image"><img alt="Ashura Studying" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/0/0a/Ashura_Studying.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20210214043904" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="180" height="111" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Ashura Studying.png" data-image-key="Ashura_Studying.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/0/0a/Ashura_Studying.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20210214043904" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Ashura_Studying.png" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Ashura studying to improve himself despite great difficulties.</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>Ashura was once an extremely violent and dangerous outlaw. He claimed that he hated people with a higher status than him. After being defeated by <a href="/wiki/Kouzuki_Oden" title="Kouzuki Oden">Kouzuki Oden</a>, who chose to spare his life and offered him a chance to live a peaceful life by rebuilding Kuri, Ashura became one of his most loyal followers out of immense gratitude. He and the other Nine Red Scabbards attempted to steal money from <a href="/wiki/Shimotsuki_Yasuie" title="Shimotsuki Yasuie">Shimotsuki Yasuie</a> to support Oden.<sup id="cite_ref-c943_16-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c943-16">&#91;16&#93;</a></sup> Ashura was even willing to study hard to improve himself on Oden's behalf.
</p><p>Ashura was an extremely loyal person, as he referred to Oden as "Oden-sama" even after his death.<sup id="cite_ref-c924p6_17-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c924p6-17">&#91;17&#93;</a></sup> His dedication was also seen when he patiently tried to assemble an army of samurai to support the <a href="/wiki/Kouzuki_Family" title="Kouzuki Family">Kouzuki Family</a> and continued to believe in Toki's prophecy ten years after her death.<sup id="cite_ref-c950_18-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c950-18">&#91;18&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>He was also courageous and almost fearless. When he encountered <a href="/wiki/Jack" title="Jack">Jack</a> in <a href="/wiki/Kuri#Okobore_Town" title="Kuri">Okobore Town</a>, the then ruler of <a href="/wiki/Kuri" title="Kuri">Kuri</a> and one of the <a href="/wiki/Beasts_Pirates" title="Beasts Pirates">Beasts Pirates</a>' All-Stars, the former was not afraid to attack the latter immediately and did not even fear Jack's reputation. However, he was cautious of <a href="/wiki/Kaidou" title="Kaidou">Kaidou</a>'s strength, but he would have fought back against him if only to create an opening for his escape.<sup id="cite_ref-c921p13_19-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c921p13-19">&#91;19&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-c922_20-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c922-20">&#91;20&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>Ashura was also a very caring person. When the samurai he had gathered tried to attack Kaidou at <a href="/wiki/Onigashima" title="Onigashima">Onigashima</a>, he cried and tried to stop them, but his words were in vain because they did not listen.<sup id="cite_ref-c950_18-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c950-18">&#91;18&#93;</a></sup> After losing the last of his comrades, Ashura finally lost hope and returned to being a criminal under the alias Shutenmaru and formed a <a href="/wiki/Mt._Atama_Thieves" title="Mt. Atama Thieves">group of thieves</a> because he was disillusioned and nihilistic towards the state of the country.
</p>
<table class="noprint" cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" border="0" style="width:100%; clear:both;">
</table><table class="noprint" cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" border="0" align="center" style="background:none; text-align:center;">
 <tbody><tr>
  <td style="vertical-align:top; font-size:3em; color:#88B7FD; font-family:&#39;Times New Roman&#39;,serif; font-weight:bold; padding:.3em 0em 0em 0em; text-shadow: 1px -1px gray;">“</td>
  <td style="padding:1em 1em; font-family:&#39;Times New Roman&#39;,serif;; font-style:italic; font-size:medium; color:inherit;">Hear that, grams? No use clinging to life. All you see around you is cruel reality. </td>
  <td style="vertical-align:bottom; font-size:3em; color:#88B7FD; font-family:&#39;Times New Roman&#39;,serif; font-weight:bold; padding-bottom:0em; padding-left:0em; padding-right:0em; text-shadow: -1px 1px gray;">”</td>
 </tr>
</tbody></table>
<table style="padding-right: 2%; font-size:80%; text-align:right; width:100%;">
 <tbody><tr valign="top">
  <td><cite style="font-family:&#39;Arial&#39;,sans-serif;">—&#160;Ashura's disillusioned view on Wano Country.<sup id="cite_ref-c921_13-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c921-13">&#91;13&#93;</a></sup></cite>
  </td>
 </tr>
</tbody></table>

<p><br />
After returning to being a criminal, he became an aggressive and prideful person. He stole from both Wano's wealthiest and poorest citizens for the same self-sufficiency motives. He also did not care what would happen to his country due to the lack of strong and noble people like Oden. As such, Ashura was disgusted with Luffy's heroism in feeding the citizens of <a href="/wiki/Okobore_Town" class="mw-redirect" title="Okobore Town">Okobore Town</a>. He also initially refused to rejoin the Kouzuki Family after they returned for their campaign to overthrow Kaidou and Orochi, accusing them of abandoning Wano Country. Ironically, his cynicism was what prevent him from falling into Kanjuro’s scheme into believing the fake Oden even though he wished it was him. Despite his callous behavior and nihilism towards the citizens of Wano, Ashura still had some compassion, as he secretly felt sympathy towards the citizens of Ebisu Town, who had lost the ability to express sadness and anger from eating the SMILEs that Orochi manipulated them into eating. He was also distraught when Yasuie was executed, showing that he still cared greatly for those that were his comrades.
</p><p>After deciding to rejoin the Nine Red Scabbards, Ashura became friendly with his comrades again, though he still bickered with them from time to time.<sup id="cite_ref-c950p13_14-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c950p13-14">&#91;14&#93;</a></sup> He ultimately chose to sacrifice himself to prevent Kanjuro's explosives from killing the other Scabbards.<sup id="cite_ref-c1008_21-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c1008-21">&#91;21&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>Ashura was one of the few samurai known to still use <a href="/wiki/Sunacchi" title="Sunacchi">Sunacchi</a>, which was once part of the old dialect of Kuri in Wano Country. Ashura and his men used it frequently amongst themselves and in battle.
</p><p>Ashura seemed to enjoy drinking alcohol.<sup id="cite_ref-c921_13-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c921-13">&#91;13&#93;</a></sup> In the past, he also drank blood from a decapitated snake.<sup id="cite_ref-c962_22-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c962-22">&#91;22&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Relationships">Relationships</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FAshura_Doji%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D4&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Allies">Allies</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FAshura_Doji%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D5&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Kouzuki_Family_and_Nine_Red_Scabbards">Kouzuki Family and Nine Red Scabbards</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FAshura_Doji%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D6&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<figure class="thumb tleft show-info-icon" style="width: 300px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/7/7f/Scabbards_Charge_Kaidou.png/revision/latest?cb=20230303041405" class="image"><img alt="Scabbards Charge Kaidou" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="300" height="169" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Scabbards Charge Kaidou.png" data-image-key="Scabbards_Charge_Kaidou.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/7/7f/Scabbards_Charge_Kaidou.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/300?cb=20230303041405" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/7/7f/Scabbards_Charge_Kaidou.png/revision/latest?cb=20230303041405" class="image"><img alt="Scabbards Charge Kaidou" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/7/7f/Scabbards_Charge_Kaidou.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/300?cb=20230303041405" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="300" height="169" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Scabbards Charge Kaidou.png" data-image-key="Scabbards_Charge_Kaidou.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/7/7f/Scabbards_Charge_Kaidou.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/300?cb=20230303041405" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Scabbards_Charge_Kaidou.png" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Ashura, alongside the other Red Scabbards (with Izou taking Kanjuro's place), charges into battle.</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>In the past, when <a href="/wiki/Kuri" title="Kuri">Kuri</a> was a lawless region, Ashura Doji was confronted by <a href="/wiki/Kouzuki_Oden" title="Kouzuki Oden">Kouzuki Oden</a>, the son of Shogun <a href="/wiki/Kouzuki_Sukiyaki" title="Kouzuki Sukiyaki">Kouzuki Sukiyaki</a>. After an entire night of intense battle, he was finally defeated. Despite wishing to die by Oden's hands as part of his own choice to live and die in violence, Oden chose to spare Ashura and reformed him by enlisting his help in bringing order to Kuri. Thus, Ashura is extremely grateful to Oden for showing him a possible future to live in peace, though he was irritated when Oden kicked him in the face when he expressed his gratitude. He and the other retainers attempted to steal money from the daimyo <a href="/wiki/Shimotsuki_Yasuie" title="Shimotsuki Yasuie">Shimotsuki Yasuie</a> to support Oden. Even after his death, Ashura still refers to him as "Oden-sama", showing undying respect and loyalty to the daimyo of Kuri.<sup id="cite_ref-c924p6_17-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c924p6-17">&#91;17&#93;</a></sup> Ashura and the other retainers also seemed to get along well.<sup id="cite_ref-c950p13_14-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c950p13-14">&#91;14&#93;</a></sup>However, after the fall of the Kouzuki Family, Ashura tried to support his allies by gathering samurai, even though it ended up in vain due to them growing impatient and attacking Onigashima, which led to their deaths. This led him to sever his ties with the Kouzuki Family.<sup id="cite_ref-c950_18-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c950-18">&#91;18&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>Later, after the missing <a href="/wiki/Nine_Red_Scabbards" title="Nine Red Scabbards">Nine Red Scabbards</a> returned, their relationship became strained. Ashura became angered and frustrated at <a href="/wiki/Kin%27emon" title="Kin&#39;emon">Kin'emon</a> and the others for having vanished for so long. Ashura said that he only respects and is loyal to someone named Oden, not to his family. In truth, he was angered because some of his comrades died in vain ten years ago. His resentment toward the family was so much that he even referred to Momonosuke, who is Oden's son, without any honorifics, resulting in Kikunojo expressing her disappointment. The closest to any camaraderie Ashura expressed was that he spared them from his banditry. However, Kin'emon made it clear that he would make Ashura their ally and had no qualms framing him for theft.<sup id="cite_ref-c925_3-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c925-3">&#91;3&#93;</a></sup> This only made Ashura angrier after he found out about it, but he was still lenient enough to listen to Kin'emon's apology and pleas. Ashura then showed Kin'emon and Inuarashi the graves of fallen comrades and explained what happened to their allies after they had lost patience in waiting for their return. Ashura finally rejoined the Scabbards and invited his bandit group to take part in the fight against Kaidou and the Beasts Pirates.<sup id="cite_ref-c950_18-3" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c950-18">&#91;18&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Mt._Atama_Thieves">Mt. Atama Thieves</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FAshura_Doji%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D7&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<p>All the members of the Mt. Atama Thieves were extremely loyal and supportive of Shutenmaru, aiding him in stealing and robbing. When Shutenmaru decided to join the Kouzuki Family's revolution, all his underlings happily agreed to join him.<sup id="cite_ref-c950_18-4" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c950-18">&#91;18&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Enemies">Enemies</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FAshura_Doji%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D8&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Beasts_Pirates">Beasts Pirates</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FAshura_Doji%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D9&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<p>Ten years ago, Ashura tried gathering forces to support the Kouzuki Family in the fight against Kaidou. However, after his comrades threw their lives away, Ashura lost hope and seemingly gave up.<sup id="cite_ref-c950_18-5" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c950-18">&#91;18&#93;</a></sup> Kaidou recognized his strength and wanted him to join his crew, but Ashura had no intention of joining and pledging loyalty to the <a href="/wiki/Beasts_Pirates" title="Beasts Pirates">Beasts Pirates</a>. However, he is well aware of Kaidou's strength and would try to avoid him whenever possible.
</p><p>Despite him being intimidated by Kaidou, he is not afraid to pick fights with the Emperor's subordinates. When Ashura encountered Jack in Okobore Town, the former did not hesitate to attack the latter and did not even fear his reputation.
</p><p>Kaidou was initially unaware of Ashura's connection with the Kouzuki Family until he saw him in person, as he only knew him as a thief called Shutenmaru.
</p>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Kurozumi_Kanjuro">Kurozumi Kanjuro</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FAshura_Doji%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D10&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<p>Ashura was previously on good terms with <a href="/wiki/Kurozumi_Kanjuro" title="Kurozumi Kanjuro">Kanjuro</a>, as they both served as faithful vassals of Oden. However, Kanjuro later revealed that he was of the <a href="/wiki/Kurozumi_Family" title="Kurozumi Family">Kurozumi Family</a>, that he was a spy sent by Orochi all along, and that he was the one who revealed the <a href="/wiki/Ninja-Pirate-Mink-Samurai_Alliance" title="Ninja-Pirate-Mink-Samurai Alliance">alliance's</a> plans to Orochi greatly shocking Ashura alongside the other Scabbards present. Ashura was angry when Kanjuro captured Momonosuke after Kin'emon failed to kill him.<sup id="cite_ref-c974_23-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c974-23">&#91;23&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>Ultimately, Ashura died to protect his fellow Scabbards from one of Kanjuro's traps when he took the full brunt of the explosion personally.
</p>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Abilities_and_Powers">Abilities and Powers</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FAshura_Doji%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D11&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Overview">Overview</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FAshura_Doji%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D12&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p>As the leader of the <a href="/wiki/Mt._Atama_Thieves" title="Mt. Atama Thieves">Mt. Atama Thieves</a>, Ashura Doji had complete authority over the group. He had excellent leadership skills, as he successfully led his bandits on missions to raid Orochi's <a href="/wiki/Paradise_Farm" title="Paradise Farm">Paradise Farm</a> multiple times, though his group eventually came under suspicion.<sup id="cite_ref-c914_24-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c914-24">&#91;24&#93;</a></sup> 25 years ago, while Oden was away with the Whitebeard Pirates, Ashura assumed control of the <a href="/wiki/Yakuza" title="Yakuza">yakuza</a> in Kuri as the new yakuza boss, and kept both the yakuza and bandits in the region from going out of control.<sup id="cite_ref-c968_6-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c968-6">&#91;6&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>Combat-wise, Ashura was a mighty samurai, once feared as the "Strongest Monster of <a href="/wiki/Kuri" title="Kuri">Kuri</a>"<span style="font-weight: normal"> (<span class="t_nihongo_kanji" lang="ja">九里最強の怪物</span><span class="t_nihongo_comma">,</span> <i><span class="t_nihongo_romaji">Kuri Saikyō no Kaibutsu</span></i><span class="t_nihongo_help"><sup><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Help:Japanese" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Help:Japanese"><span class="t_nihongo_icon" style="color:#00e;font:bold 80% sans-serif;text-decoration:none;padding:0 .1em;">?</span></a></sup></span>)</span>—the most dangerous villain frequenting said region during its era of chaos—until he was defeated by Oden four decades ago (the latter taking a whole night to take down both Ashura and his then-cohorts).<sup id="cite_ref-c962_22-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c962-22">&#91;22&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-debut_1-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-debut-1">&#91;1&#93;</a></sup> Even more, in the last 20 years, Ashura claims to have become stronger.<sup id="cite_ref-c950_18-6" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c950-18">&#91;18&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p><a href="/wiki/Kin%27emon" title="Kin&#39;emon">Kin'emon</a> hailed Ashura as one of the strongest Scabbards (alongside <a href="/wiki/Kawamatsu" title="Kawamatsu">Kawamatsu</a> and <a href="/wiki/Denjiro" title="Denjiro">Denjiro</a>) and worth 100 men in battle.<sup id="cite_ref-c921_13-3" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c921-13">&#91;13&#93;</a></sup> <a href="/wiki/Kaidou" title="Kaidou">Kaidou</a> himself, an <a href="/wiki/Four_Emperors" title="Four Emperors">Emperor</a>, sought to recruit him<sup id="cite_ref-c921p13_19-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c921p13-19">&#91;19&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-c922_20-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c922-20">&#91;20&#93;</a></sup> and <a href="/wiki/Holed%27em" title="Holed&#39;em">Holed'em</a>, a <a href="/wiki/Beasts_Pirates#Shinuchi" title="Beasts Pirates">Shinuchi</a> of the <a href="/wiki/Beasts_Pirates" title="Beasts Pirates">Beasts Pirates</a>, surmised that <a href="/wiki/Monkey_D._Luffy" title="Monkey D. Luffy">Monkey D. Luffy</a> must have been Ashura's subordinate going by his power.<sup id="cite_ref-alias_5-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-alias-5">&#91;5&#93;</a></sup> Perhaps most impressively, Ashura was able to fight evenly against the <a href="/wiki/Beasts_Pirates#All-Stars" title="Beasts Pirates">All-Star</a> <a href="/wiki/Jack" title="Jack">Jack</a>, a top henchman of Kaidou with a bounty of <span style="white-space:nowrap;"><a href="/wiki/Belly" title="Belly"><img alt="Beli" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="12" height="20" data-image-name="Beli.png" data-image-key="Beli.png" data-relevant="0" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/d/de/Beli.png/revision/latest?cb=20141206091723" class="lazyload" /></a></span>1,000,000,000, even dealing him a severe wound,<sup id="cite_ref-c921_13-4" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c921-13">&#91;13&#93;</a></sup> and fought evenly with <a href="/wiki/Inuarashi" title="Inuarashi">Inuarashi</a>, one of the two strongest warriors of the <a href="/wiki/Mink_Tribe" title="Mink Tribe">Mink Tribe</a>, in a sparring match.<sup id="cite_ref-c925_3-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c925-3">&#91;3&#93;</a></sup> However, Ashura was well aware that he had no chance against Kaidou by himself, preferring to retreat when faced with him a second time.<sup id="cite_ref-c922_20-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c922-20">&#91;20&#93;</a></sup> By combining his power with that of three other Scabbards, he was able to seriously injure Kaidou in his <a href="/wiki/Uo_Uo_no_Mi,_Model:_Seiryu" title="Uo Uo no Mi, Model: Seiryu">dragon form</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-c992p16_25-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c992p16-25">&#91;25&#93;</a></sup> 
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Physical_Abilities">Physical Abilities</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FAshura_Doji%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D13&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p>Ashura was capable of applying tremendous physical power to his swordsmanship, as he matched Inuarashi and Jack in strength, even giving the latter a massive wound across his chest.<sup id="cite_ref-c921_13-5" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c921-13">&#91;13&#93;</a></sup> Alongside his fellow Scabbards, Ashura managed to push <a href="/wiki/Kaidou" title="Kaidou">Kaidou</a> off his feet when ambushing him.<sup id="cite_ref-26" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-26">&#91;26&#93;</a></sup> Even after being brutally defeated by Kaidou, he retained enough strength to tackle Kanjuro's drawing of Oden through a wall.<sup id="cite_ref-c1008_21-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c1008-21">&#91;21&#93;</a></sup> Despite his large build, Ashura was extremely fast, as shown when he charged toward <a href="/wiki/Jack" title="Jack">Jack</a> in an instant.<sup id="cite_ref-c921_13-6" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c921-13">&#91;13&#93;</a></sup> Ashura had great endurance and a tolerance for pain, as he was seemingly unaffected when Jack cut him on the shoulder and survived being stabbed in the back by <a href="/wiki/King" title="King">King</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-c921_13-7" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c921-13">&#91;13&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-27" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-27">&#91;27&#93;</a></sup> Similarly, he quickly recovered after being impaled by Kanjuro's drawing and exhibited no discomfort as he was stabbed multiple times.<sup id="cite_ref-28" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-28">&#91;28&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Swordsmanship">Swordsmanship</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FAshura_Doji%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D14&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<dl><dd><i>Further information: <a href="/wiki/Oden_Two_Sword_Style" title="Oden Two Sword Style">Oden Two Sword Style</a></i></dd></dl>
<figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 220px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/3/39/Scabbards_Use_Oden_Two_Sword_Style.png/revision/latest?cb=20220621131809" class="image"><img alt="Scabbards Use Oden Two Sword Style" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="220" height="124" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Scabbards Use Oden Two Sword Style.png" data-image-key="Scabbards_Use_Oden_Two_Sword_Style.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/3/39/Scabbards_Use_Oden_Two_Sword_Style.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/220?cb=20220621131809" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/3/39/Scabbards_Use_Oden_Two_Sword_Style.png/revision/latest?cb=20220621131809" class="image"><img alt="Scabbards Use Oden Two Sword Style" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/3/39/Scabbards_Use_Oden_Two_Sword_Style.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/220?cb=20220621131809" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="220" height="124" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Scabbards Use Oden Two Sword Style.png" data-image-key="Scabbards_Use_Oden_Two_Sword_Style.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/3/39/Scabbards_Use_Oden_Two_Sword_Style.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/220?cb=20220621131809" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Scabbards_Use_Oden_Two_Sword_Style.png" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Ashura, alongside three other Scabbards, wields Oden Two Sword Style against Kaidou.</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>Ashura was a highly skilled and powerful swordsman. With one slash, he gave Jack a large cut across his chest and broke one of his shotel blades. He then proceeded to fight evenly with the pirate in what spectators considered to be a high-level duel.<sup id="cite_ref-c921_13-8" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c921-13">&#91;13&#93;</a></sup> He was capable of emulating Oden's signature <b>Oden Two Sword Style</b> style, allowing him to wield two swords at the same time and perform one of his techniques.<sup id="cite_ref-c992p16_25-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c992p16-25">&#91;25&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Haki">Haki</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FAshura_Doji%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D15&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<dl><dd><div class="noprint"><i>Main article&#58; <a href="/wiki/Haki" title="Haki">Haki</a></i></div></dd></dl>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Armament_Haki">Armament Haki</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FAshura_Doji%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D16&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<p>Ashura was a master of <a href="/wiki/Haki/Armament_Haki" title="Haki/Armament Haki">Armament Haki</a>, known as "Ryuo" in Wano. He could harden his swords and also possessed an advanced level of this Haki, as shown when he cut through Kaidou's tremendously tough skin.<sup id="cite_ref-c992p16_25-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c992p16-25">&#91;25&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Observation_Haki">Observation Haki</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FAshura_Doji%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D17&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<p>Ashura possessed the ability to use <a href="/wiki/Haki/Observation_Haki" title="Haki/Observation Haki">Observation Haki</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-vivre_card_9-3" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-vivre_card-9">&#91;9&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="History">History</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FAshura_Doji%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D18&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Past">Past</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FAshura_Doji%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D19&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<figure class="thumb tleft show-info-icon" style="width: 200px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/c/cc/Oden_Defeats_Ashura.png/revision/latest?cb=20210214034612" class="image"><img alt="Oden Defeats Ashura" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="200" height="122" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Oden Defeats Ashura.png" data-image-key="Oden_Defeats_Ashura.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/c/cc/Oden_Defeats_Ashura.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/200?cb=20210214034612" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/c/cc/Oden_Defeats_Ashura.png/revision/latest?cb=20210214034612" class="image"><img alt="Oden Defeats Ashura" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/c/cc/Oden_Defeats_Ashura.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/200?cb=20210214034612" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="200" height="122" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Oden Defeats Ashura.png" data-image-key="Oden_Defeats_Ashura.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/c/cc/Oden_Defeats_Ashura.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/200?cb=20210214034612" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Oden_Defeats_Ashura.png" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Ashura and his goons defeated by Oden.</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>Many years ago, Ashura Doji was the most dangerous criminal in the lawless region of <a href="/wiki/Kuri" title="Kuri">Kuri</a>. When he heard that <a href="/wiki/Kouzuki_Oden" title="Kouzuki Oden">Kouzuki Oden</a> was coming to Kuri, Ashura eagerly waited for him. After Oden eventually arrived at Kuri, they clashed and Ashura was defeated after a day of intense fighting.<sup id="cite_ref-c962_22-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c962-22">&#91;22&#93;</a></sup> After Oden became <a href="/wiki/Daimyo" title="Daimyo">daimyo</a> of Kuri, Ashura became one of his retainers.<sup id="cite_ref-29" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-29">&#91;29&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>After <a href="/wiki/Inuarashi" title="Inuarashi">Inuarashi</a>, <a href="/wiki/Nekomamushi" title="Nekomamushi">Nekomamushi</a>, and <a href="/wiki/Kawamatsu" title="Kawamatsu">Kawamatsu</a> joined Oden, they were running low on funds. Therefore, he and the other retainers attempted to steal money from <a href="/wiki/Shimotsuki_Yasuie" title="Shimotsuki Yasuie">Shimotsuki Yasuie</a>, but they were caught. Instead of punishing them, Yasuie allowed them to take the money and encouraged them to use it to become better people for the sake of Oden and <a href="/wiki/Wano_Country" title="Wano Country">Wano Country</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-c943_16-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c943-16">&#91;16&#93;</a></sup> Following Yasuie's advice, they educated themselves and trained to become dignified warriors. 30 years ago, they visited the <a href="/wiki/Flower_Capital" title="Flower Capital">Flower Capital</a> with Oden.<sup id="cite_ref-30" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-30">&#91;30&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>After meeting the <a href="/wiki/Whitebeard_Pirates" title="Whitebeard Pirates">Whitebeard Pirates</a>, Oden and his retainers were having a feast with them. When the Whitebeard Pirates left Wano two weeks later, the retainers discovered Oden, <a href="/wiki/Izou" title="Izou">Izou</a>, Inuarashi, and Nekomamushi to be missing.<sup id="cite_ref-31" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-31">&#91;31&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>While Oden was away, Ashura lead the <a href="/wiki/Yakuza" title="Yakuza">yakuza</a> and the <a href="/wiki/Bandits" title="Bandits">bandits</a> in Kuri to keep them from going out of control.<sup id="cite_ref-c968_6-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c968-6">&#91;6&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>After Oden failed to kill the new <a href="/wiki/Shogun" title="Shogun">shogun</a>, <a href="/wiki/Kurozumi_Orochi" title="Kurozumi Orochi">Kurozumi Orochi</a>, 25 years ago, the retainers remained loyal to him for the next five years despite Oden acting like a fool and losing the respect of most of Wano's people. 20 years ago, Oden finally had enough and decided to take down <a href="/wiki/Kaidou" title="Kaidou">Kaidou</a>. The <a href="/wiki/Nine_Red_Scabbards" title="Nine Red Scabbards">Nine Red Scabbards</a> eagerly followed him and marched with him to <a href="/wiki/Onigashima" title="Onigashima">Onigashima</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-32" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-32">&#91;32&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>On the way to Onigashima, the group was confronted by Kaidou and his <a href="/wiki/Beasts_Pirates" title="Beasts Pirates">crew</a> in the <a href="/wiki/Udon" title="Udon">Udon</a> region. In the ensuing battle, the <a href="/wiki/Samurai" title="Samurai">samurai</a> were joined by <a href="/wiki/Shinobu" title="Shinobu">Shinobu</a>. After seeing Oden struck down by Kaidou, Ashura was stabbed in the back. Unfortunately, the samurai were overwhelmed in the end. Oden and the Scabbards were then imprisoned in the Flower Capital and sentenced to be boiled alive in three days.<sup id="cite_ref-33" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-33">&#91;33&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 200px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/d/d7/Kaidou_vs_Red_Scabbards.png/revision/latest?cb=20191208071646" class="image"><img alt="Kaidou vs Red Scabbards" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="200" height="112" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Kaidou vs Red Scabbards.png" data-image-key="Kaidou_vs_Red_Scabbards.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/d/d7/Kaidou_vs_Red_Scabbards.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/200?cb=20191208071646" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/d/d7/Kaidou_vs_Red_Scabbards.png/revision/latest?cb=20191208071646" class="image"><img alt="Kaidou vs Red Scabbards" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/d/d7/Kaidou_vs_Red_Scabbards.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/200?cb=20191208071646" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="200" height="112" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Kaidou vs Red Scabbards.png" data-image-key="Kaidou_vs_Red_Scabbards.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/d/d7/Kaidou_vs_Red_Scabbards.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/200?cb=20191208071646" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Kaidou_vs_Red_Scabbards.png" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Ashura and Denjiro face Kaidou.</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>All ten prisoners were later brought to the execution site, at which point Oden made a deal with Kaidou. After Oden stepped into the pot of boiling oil, the retainers were about to join him, but Oden grabbed a plank and ordered them to stand on it as he held them over the pot.<sup id="cite_ref-34" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-34">&#91;34&#93;</a></sup> As Oden endured the <a href="/wiki/Legendary_Hour" title="Legendary Hour">hour</a>, he explained to his retainers the reason Wano Country was isolated and requested them to open Wano's borders for him. Oden successfully survived the hour, but Orochi summoned a firing squad to execute Oden and his retainers. Oden once again told his retainers to open Wano's borders before throwing them far away from the pot. The Scabbards fled with tears as Oden met his demise.<sup id="cite_ref-35" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-35">&#91;35&#93;</a></sup> As they were chased by an army of pursuers, Shinobu gave the Scabbards their <a href="/wiki/Weapons" title="Weapons">weapons</a>. After Inuarashi and Nekomamushi were caught, Ashura and <a href="/wiki/Denjiro" title="Denjiro">Denjiro</a> split from the rest of the group to fight their enemies.<sup id="cite_ref-36" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-36">&#91;36&#93;</a></sup> At some point, Ashura and Denjiro fought Kaidou. Ashura was able to escape and hid in the mountains.
</p>
<figure class="thumb tleft show-info-icon" style="width: 210px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/3/35/Ashura%27s_Comrades_Suicide_Mission.png/revision/latest?cb=20201115032307" class="image"><img alt="Ashura&#39;s Comrades Suicide Mission" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="210" height="118" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Ashura&#39;s Comrades Suicide Mission.png" data-image-key="Ashura%27s_Comrades_Suicide_Mission.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/3/35/Ashura%27s_Comrades_Suicide_Mission.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20201115032307" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/3/35/Ashura%27s_Comrades_Suicide_Mission.png/revision/latest?cb=20201115032307" class="image"><img alt="Ashura&#39;s Comrades Suicide Mission" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/3/35/Ashura%27s_Comrades_Suicide_Mission.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20201115032307" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="210" height="118" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Ashura&#39;s Comrades Suicide Mission.png" data-image-key="Ashura%27s_Comrades_Suicide_Mission.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/3/35/Ashura%27s_Comrades_Suicide_Mission.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20201115032307" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Ashura%27s_Comrades_Suicide_Mission.png" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Ashura watches his comrades sail to their doom while he hopelessly tries to stop them.</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>Ten years after Oden's death, Ashura had many friends who became too eager to fight Kaidou and Orochi and did not fully believe <a href="/wiki/Kouzuki_Toki" title="Kouzuki Toki">Toki</a>'s prophecy about the <a href="/wiki/Toki_Toki_no_Mi" title="Toki Toki no Mi">return</a> of the missing Red Scabbards. Thus, they impatiently went straight to Onigashima to fight Kaidou. Ashura tried to stop them from throwing their lives away, but these words were in vain, and his comrades ultimately perished at the hands of Kaidou.<sup id="cite_ref-c950_18-7" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c950-18">&#91;18&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>Distraught at his comrades' pointless demise, Ashura eventually lost hope, went back to being a criminal, and adopted the alias Shutenmaru.<sup id="cite_ref-c924p8_11-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c924p8-11">&#91;11&#93;</a></sup> He also formed the <a href="/wiki/Mt._Atama_Thieves" title="Mt. Atama Thieves">Mt. Atama Thieves</a>. At some point, he encountered Kaidou, in which Kaidou wanted him to be part of his crew.<sup id="cite_ref-c922_20-3" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c922-20">&#91;20&#93;</a></sup> Ashura also managed to acquire the blueprints of Kaidou's fortress within the <a href="/wiki/Skull_Dome" title="Skull Dome">Skull Dome</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-37" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-37">&#91;37&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>A few weeks before <a href="/wiki/Monkey_D._Luffy" title="Monkey D. Luffy">Monkey D. Luffy</a>'s arrival at Wano Country, Ashura and other thieves managed to steal <a href="/wiki/Foods" title="Foods">food</a> from the <a href="/wiki/Paradise_Farm" title="Paradise Farm">farm</a> that Oden had established, which was now owned by Orochi.<sup id="cite_ref-c914_24-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c914-24">&#91;24&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Wano_Country_Saga">Wano Country Saga</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FAshura_Doji%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D20&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Wano_Country_Arc">Wano Country Arc</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FAshura_Doji%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D21&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 200px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/6/68/Shutenmaru_Attacks_Jack.png/revision/latest?cb=20181123210643" class="image"><img alt="Shutenmaru Attacks Jack" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="200" height="225" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Shutenmaru Attacks Jack.png" data-image-key="Shutenmaru_Attacks_Jack.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/6/68/Shutenmaru_Attacks_Jack.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/200?cb=20181123210643" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/6/68/Shutenmaru_Attacks_Jack.png/revision/latest?cb=20181123210643" class="image"><img alt="Shutenmaru Attacks Jack" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/6/68/Shutenmaru_Attacks_Jack.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/200?cb=20181123210643" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="200" height="225" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Shutenmaru Attacks Jack.png" data-image-key="Shutenmaru_Attacks_Jack.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/6/68/Shutenmaru_Attacks_Jack.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/200?cb=20181123210643" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Shutenmaru_Attacks_Jack.png" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Ashura Doji attacks Jack.</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>Ashura and his thieves came to Okobore Town, where they stole the fresh food that Luffy had given to the residents there. He was confronted by an old woman who believed that the samurai would return to protect them, and in response, Ashura prepared to attack her. However, before he could, he was confronted by <a href="/wiki/Jack" title="Jack">Jack</a> of the <a href="/wiki/Beasts_Pirates" title="Beasts Pirates">Beasts Pirates</a>. Jack asked about the <a href="/wiki/Straw_Hat_Pirates" title="Straw Hat Pirates">Straw Hat Pirates</a> and mentioned that Ashura had only been left alive because <a href="/wiki/Kaidou" title="Kaidou">Kaidou</a> wanted him as his subordinate. He reiterated that he would never join them and then attacked Jack with a massive cut, causing the two to begin fighting. Jack managed to wound Ashura, but he was unwavering. However, their duel was interrupted when Kaidou came flying in to tell Jack to bring the Straw Hats to him.<sup id="cite_ref-38" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-38">&#91;38&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>Ashura and his gang then began retreating to the forest. Kaidou spotted him and asked him to become his subordinate. Ashura prepared for a fight, but <a href="/wiki/Basil_Hawkins" title="Basil Hawkins">Basil Hawkins</a> drew Kaidou's attention to Oden Castle. The thief was then angry at Kaidou for destroying the castle ruins,<sup id="cite_ref-c922_20-4" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c922-20">&#91;20&#93;</a></sup> and after Luffy attacked Kaidou, Ashura told his men to retreat to the mountain before watching Luffy's futile attempt to defeat Kaidou.<sup id="cite_ref-39" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-39">&#91;39&#93;</a></sup> After Kaidou defeated Luffy, Ashura saw the unconscious Luffy knocking out some of the <a href="/wiki/Four_Emperors" title="Four Emperors">Emperor</a>'s subordinates with <a href="/wiki/Haki/Supreme_King_Haki" title="Haki/Supreme King Haki">Supreme King Haki</a> and realized he had the same power as Oden. He then departed from Okobore Town.<sup id="cite_ref-40" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-40">&#91;40&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<figure class="thumb tleft show-info-icon" style="width: 200px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/e/ec/Shutenmaru_vs._Inuarashi.png/revision/latest?cb=20230302155520" class="image"><img alt="Shutenmaru vs" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="200" height="141" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Shutenmaru vs. Inuarashi.png" data-image-key="Shutenmaru_vs._Inuarashi.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/e/ec/Shutenmaru_vs._Inuarashi.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/200?cb=20230302155520" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/e/ec/Shutenmaru_vs._Inuarashi.png/revision/latest?cb=20230302155520" class="image"><img alt="Shutenmaru vs" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/e/ec/Shutenmaru_vs._Inuarashi.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/200?cb=20230302155520" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="200" height="141" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Shutenmaru vs. Inuarashi.png" data-image-key="Shutenmaru_vs._Inuarashi.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/e/ec/Shutenmaru_vs._Inuarashi.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/200?cb=20230302155520" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Shutenmaru_vs._Inuarashi.png" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Ashura clashes with Inuarashi as he refuses to help the Kouzuki Family again.</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>At Mt. Atama, Ashura clashed with Inuarashi, but the fight was interrupted by <a href="/wiki/Kin%27emon" title="Kin&#39;emon">Kin'emon</a>. Ashura stated that while he admired Oden, he never swore loyalty to the entire <a href="/wiki/Kouzuki_Family" title="Kouzuki Family">Kouzuki Family</a>. However, Kin'emon ignored this claim and emphasized that he was determined to make Ashura their ally once again.<sup id="cite_ref-c925_3-3" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c925-3">&#91;3&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>Sometime later, Mt. Atama was set on fire by one of <a href="/wiki/Holed%27em" title="Holed&#39;em">Holed'em</a>'s subordinates. Enraged, Ashura decided to go to Bakura Town to retaliate.<sup id="cite_ref-41" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-41">&#91;41&#93;</a></sup> He and his gang later entered Bakura Town and witnessed <a href="/wiki/Shimotsuki_Yasuie" title="Shimotsuki Yasuie">Shimotsuki Yasuie</a>'s execution on the broadcast.<sup id="cite_ref-42" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-42">&#91;42&#93;</a></sup> After the execution, he was the only one of the <a href="/wiki/Nine_Red_Scabbards" title="Nine Red Scabbards">Nine Red Scabbards</a> to hold his tears after Yasuie's death, and thereafter asked Kin'emon and Inuarashi if they knew about the <a href="/wiki/SMILE" title="SMILE">SMILE</a> fruits.<sup id="cite_ref-43" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-43">&#91;43&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>Outside Bakura Town, Ashura learned that Kin'emon framed him for theft. He got angry and knocked Kin'emon to the ground. Kin'emon and Inuarashi apologized and once again asked Ashura to join them. Ashura then told Kin'emon and Inuarashi to follow him, wanting to show them something.<sup id="cite_ref-44" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-44">&#91;44&#93;</a></sup> When they arrived, Ashura showed them the graves of their dead comrades and explained what had happened to their allies ten years ago. He recounted how they had all lost patience and had tried to fight Kaidou, but were all killed in battle. Ashura then determined that it was time for him to rejoin his comrades to avenge those who had fallen and to also overthrow Kaidou and Orochi to restore the position of the Kouzuki Family. Inuarashi and he then rejoiced and bragged to Kin'emon about how they had twenty years more fighting experience than him now. Upon being called a duo of geezers by Kin'emon, the three began arguing, much to the worry of Ashura's henchmen.<sup id="cite_ref-c950_18-8" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c950-18">&#91;18&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>Ashura later took Kin'emon and Inuarashi to an abandoned port and showed them ships that could carry their troops to Onigashima.<sup id="cite_ref-45" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-45">&#91;45&#93;</a></sup> Ashura then gave Kin'emon the blueprints of Kaidou's residence. While Kin'emon was speaking to <a href="/wiki/Raizo" title="Raizo">Raizo</a> via <a href="/wiki/Animal_Species/Wano_Country_Saga#Smart_Tanishi" title="Animal Species/Wano Country Saga">Smart Tanishi</a>, Ashura was surprised to hear the number of allies Raizo's group gained at Udon.<sup id="cite_ref-46" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-46">&#91;46&#93;</a></sup> He later joined a meeting with several key alliance members at Amigasa Village.<sup id="cite_ref-47" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-47">&#91;47&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>Ashura then heard from <a href="/wiki/Roronoa_Zoro" title="Roronoa Zoro">Roronoa Zoro</a> and <a href="/wiki/Kawamatsu" title="Kawamatsu">Kawamatsu</a> that <a href="/wiki/Kouzuki_Hiyori" title="Kouzuki Hiyori">Kouzuki Hiyori</a> is alive. On the day for the raid on Onigashima, Ashura marched to the rebel meeting place with <a href="/wiki/Kouzuki_Momonosuke" title="Kouzuki Momonosuke">Kouzuki Momonosuke</a>, Kin'emon, <a href="/wiki/Kurozumi_Kanjuro" title="Kurozumi Kanjuro">Kanjuro</a>, Raizo, <a href="/wiki/Kikunojo" title="Kikunojo">Kikunojo</a>, Shinobu, Inuarashi, and Kawamatsu.<sup id="cite_ref-48" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-48">&#91;48&#93;</a></sup> However, the group was shocked to see that Tokage Port was destroyed and none of their allies were there.<sup id="cite_ref-49" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-49">&#91;49&#93;</a></sup> In spite of this major setback, the Scabbards were still determined to go through with the raid, knowing that they would not get another chance.<sup id="cite_ref-50" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-50">&#91;50&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>The Scabbards set sail and left Momonosuke at the port. As Kin'emon wondered about the possibility of a traitor among them, Kanjuro then revealed that he was the mole, leaving the other Scabbards stunned at this revelation. After Kanjuro explained what he did, Kin'emon angrily beheaded him, only to learn that it was a copy and the real Kanjuro remained on the coast and that he had captured Momonosuke to bring him to Onigashima. As this was happening, the Scabbards' boat was confronted by three Beasts Pirates' ships, but the ships were suddenly attacked by the Straw Hats, <a href="/wiki/Heart_Pirates" title="Heart Pirates">Heart Pirates</a>, and <a href="/wiki/Kid_Pirates" title="Kid Pirates">Kid Pirates</a>. The Scabbards' boat was then lifted by <a href="/wiki/Polar_Tang" title="Polar Tang">Law's submarine</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-51" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-51">&#91;51&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>When Kyoshiro arrived, the Scabbards were confused to see him attacking one of the Beasts Pirates' ships. They were then shocked when Kyoshiro revealed himself to be Denjiro and that he freed the prisoners in the Flower Capital and the rebels gathered at Habu Port. To their relief, the <a href="/wiki/Ninja-Pirate-Mink-Samurai_Alliance" title="Ninja-Pirate-Mink-Samurai Alliance">Ninja-Pirate-Mink-Samurai Alliance</a> allies arrived at Tokage Port on a massive fleet to commence the raid on Onigashima.<sup id="cite_ref-52" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-52">&#91;52&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>Kanjuro then fled the scene with Momonosuke in tow on a drawn crane and briefly attacked the alliance with an ink cloud that rained down ink arrows. Momonosuke ordered the alliance to press forward to Onigashima without worrying about him. As the alliance was attacked by a Beasts Pirates' ship with long ranged cannons, <a href="/wiki/Jinbe" title="Jinbe">Jinbe</a> came to aid the rebels.<sup id="cite_ref-53" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-53">&#91;53&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>After <a href="/wiki/Shishilian" title="Shishilian">Shishilian</a> and <a href="/wiki/Hyougoro" title="Hyougoro">Hyougoro</a> boarded the Polar Tang, the Scabbards discussed with <a href="/wiki/Trafalgar_D._Water_Law" title="Trafalgar D. Water Law">Trafalgar Law</a> about the plan to enter Onigashima.<sup id="cite_ref-54" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-54">&#91;54&#93;</a></sup> After the Straw Hats defeated the guards at the torii gates, the Heart Pirates and the Scabbards (except Kin'emon and Denjiro) traversed to the back of Onigashima inside the Polar Tang.<sup id="cite_ref-55" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-55">&#91;55&#93;</a></sup> Along the way, they were contacted by Nekomamushi, who just arrived and was planning to meet them at Onigashima.<sup id="cite_ref-56" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-56">&#91;56&#93;</a></sup> When the submarine got close enough, Law <a href="/wiki/Ope_Ope_no_Mi" title="Ope Ope no Mi">teleported</a> himself and the Scabbards with him to Onigashima's back entrance, where they were joined up by <a href="/wiki/Marco" title="Marco">Marco</a>, Nekomamushi, and <a href="/wiki/Izou" title="Izou">Izou</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-57" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-57">&#91;57&#93;</a></sup> After Marco left to check on a shadow he saw at sea, the group was confronted by Kanjuro and an army of Beasts Pirates. While Kikunojo clashed against Kanjuro, the rest fought the other enemies.<sup id="cite_ref-58" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-58">&#91;58&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 200px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/a/a5/Scabbards_Attack_Kaidou.png/revision/latest?cb=20231121020441" class="image"><img alt="Scabbards Attack Kaidou" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="200" height="216" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Scabbards Attack Kaidou.png" data-image-key="Scabbards_Attack_Kaidou.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/a/a5/Scabbards_Attack_Kaidou.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/200?cb=20231121020441" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/a/a5/Scabbards_Attack_Kaidou.png/revision/latest?cb=20231121020441" class="image"><img alt="Scabbards Attack Kaidou" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/a/a5/Scabbards_Attack_Kaidou.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/200?cb=20231121020441" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="200" height="216" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Scabbards Attack Kaidou.png" data-image-key="Scabbards_Attack_Kaidou.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/a/a5/Scabbards_Attack_Kaidou.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/200?cb=20231121020441" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Scabbards_Attack_Kaidou.png" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">The Scabbards attack Kaidou.</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>Kanjuro and the Beasts Pirates with him were defeated, and Ashura's group were soon rejoined by Kin'emon and Denjiro. They then entered Kaidou's castle, fought their way to the Performance Stage, and launched an all-out attack on Kaidou.<sup id="cite_ref-59" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-59">&#91;59&#93;</a></sup> While falling to the lower floor, the Scabbards managed to inflict wounds on Kaidou. As the alliance revealed themselves and attacked the Beasts Pirates, Kaidou transformed into <a href="/wiki/Uo_Uo_no_Mi,_Model:_Seiryu" title="Uo Uo no Mi, Model: Seiryu">his dragon form</a> and flew to the roof of the Skull Dome, with the Scabbards grabbing onto him. On the roof, the Scabbards prepared to fight Kaidou with the <a href="/wiki/Mink_Tribe" title="Mink Tribe">Mink Tribe</a>'s help.<sup id="cite_ref-60" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-60">&#91;60&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>Jack and a platoon arrived at the roof to assist Kaidou, and the Scabbards watched as the <a href="/wiki/Sulong" title="Sulong">Sulong</a> minks engaged the enemy.<sup id="cite_ref-61" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-61">&#91;61&#93;</a></sup> After Jack and his forces were rendered unable to battle thanks to the minks' efforts, the Scabbards resumed their confrontation with Kaidou.<sup id="cite_ref-62" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-62">&#91;62&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<figure class="thumb tleft show-info-icon" style="width: 200px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/1/10/Scabbards_Strike_Kaidou%27s_Scar.png/revision/latest?cb=20230313024406" class="image"><img alt="Scabbards Strike Kaidou&#39;s Scar" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="200" height="113" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Scabbards Strike Kaidou&#39;s Scar.png" data-image-key="Scabbards_Strike_Kaidou%27s_Scar.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/1/10/Scabbards_Strike_Kaidou%27s_Scar.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/200?cb=20230313024406" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/1/10/Scabbards_Strike_Kaidou%27s_Scar.png/revision/latest?cb=20230313024406" class="image"><img alt="Scabbards Strike Kaidou&#39;s Scar" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/1/10/Scabbards_Strike_Kaidou%27s_Scar.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/200?cb=20230313024406" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="200" height="113" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Scabbards Strike Kaidou&#39;s Scar.png" data-image-key="Scabbards_Strike_Kaidou%27s_Scar.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/1/10/Scabbards_Strike_Kaidou%27s_Scar.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/200?cb=20230313024406" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Scabbards_Strike_Kaidou%27s_Scar.png" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Ashura and three other Scabbards slash Kaidou's scar.</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>Kaidou roared lightning at them, but they dodged around it and each struck him in turn. After Raizo reflected Kaidou's Bolo Breath back at him, four of the Scabbards—Ashura, Denjiro, Kin'emon, and Inuarashi—replicated <a href="/wiki/Oden_Two_Sword_Style" title="Oden Two Sword Style">Oden's Two Sword Style</a> stance and struck Kaidou's scar with the same attack that made it.<sup id="cite_ref-63" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-63">&#91;63&#93;</a></sup> Kaidou then retaliated with a roar that created wind scythes aimed at the Scabbards.<sup id="cite_ref-64" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-64">&#91;64&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>Continuing the battle in human form, Kaidou began overwhelming the Scabbards<sup id="cite_ref-65" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-65">&#91;65&#93;</a></sup> and later incapacitated them. <a href="/wiki/Charlotte_Linlin" title="Charlotte Linlin">Big Mom</a>, <a href="/wiki/Eustass_Kid" title="Eustass Kid">Eustass Kid</a>, Killer, Zoro, Luffy, and Law later arrived at the roof. Upon Luffy's request, Law teleported the Scabbards to a safe place.<sup id="cite_ref-66" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-66">&#91;66&#93;</a></sup> They were placed in the treasure room on the second floor, where Hiyori, who had previously infiltraded Onigashima, tended to them.<sup id="cite_ref-67" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-67">&#91;67&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 190px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/1/17/Ashura_Doji%27s_Sacrifice.png/revision/latest?cb=20220821011057" class="image"><img alt="Ashura Doji&#39;s Sacrifice" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="190" height="107" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Ashura Doji&#39;s Sacrifice.png" data-image-key="Ashura_Doji%27s_Sacrifice.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/1/17/Ashura_Doji%27s_Sacrifice.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/190?cb=20220821011057" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/1/17/Ashura_Doji%27s_Sacrifice.png/revision/latest?cb=20220821011057" class="image"><img alt="Ashura Doji&#39;s Sacrifice" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/1/17/Ashura_Doji%27s_Sacrifice.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/190?cb=20220821011057" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="190" height="107" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Ashura Doji&#39;s Sacrifice.png" data-image-key="Ashura_Doji%27s_Sacrifice.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/1/17/Ashura_Doji%27s_Sacrifice.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/190?cb=20220821011057" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Ashura_Doji%27s_Sacrifice.png" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Ashura lies dead after sacrificing himself.</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>The Scabbards later recovered and regained consciousness, but the mysterious figure already had left. Before they left the treasure room, they were shockingly greeted by what appeared to be Oden.<sup id="cite_ref-68" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-68">&#91;68&#93;</a></sup> However, Ashura immediately suspected that this was an impostor and told this to his comrades who believed it was legitimate. When Kin'emon tried arguing against this, Ashura punched him out of the way while unsheathing his sword and cut "Oden" in the face. Oden did not bleed after the cut, causing the Scabbards to realize that it was one of Kanjuro's drawings, and the drawing stabbed Ashura through the chest with one of its swords. Ashura briefly laid on the ground while the Oden drawing clashed with Denjiro and spoke on Kanjuro's behalf, but then the drawing lit some <a href="/wiki/Explosive" title="Explosive">explosives</a> under its garment. Ashura immediately took action and tackled the Oden drawing, sending both of them crashing out of the room, and told his comrades to stop Kanjuro from going after Momonosuke. Ashura maintained his grip on the drawing even as it stabbed him, and the explosives then detonated, engulfing both of them in a massive explosion, which killed Ashura.<sup id="cite_ref-c1008_21-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c1008-21">&#91;21&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-c1052_15-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c1052-15">&#91;15&#93;</a></sup><br style="clear:both;" />
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Legacy">Legacy</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FAshura_Doji%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D22&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p>The explosion which took Ashura's life would inadvertently create a hole in the ceiling of the courtyard of <a href="/wiki/Onigashima" title="Onigashima">Onigashima</a>, which would later help expose <a href="/wiki/Inuarashi" title="Inuarashi">Inuarashi</a> to the <a href="/wiki/Moon" title="Moon">moonlight</a> allowing him to use his <a href="/wiki/Sulong" title="Sulong">Sulong</a> form<sup id="cite_ref-69" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-69">&#91;69&#93;</a></sup> to defeat <a href="/wiki/Jack" title="Jack">Jack</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-70" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-70">&#91;70&#93;</a></sup> Following the success of the <a href="/wiki/Raid_on_Onigashima" title="Raid on Onigashima">raid on Onigashima</a>, Kin'emon expressed a desire to build a temple in <a href="/wiki/Ringo" title="Ringo">Ringo</a> that would honor Ashura alongside Oden, <a href="/wiki/Shimotsuki_Yasuie" title="Shimotsuki Yasuie">Yasuie</a>, and <a href="/wiki/Izou" title="Izou">Izou</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-c1052_15-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c1052-15">&#91;15&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Major_Battles">Major Battles</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FAshura_Doji%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D23&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<ul><li>Ashura Doji vs. <a href="/wiki/Kouzuki_Oden" title="Kouzuki Oden">Kouzuki Oden</a></li>
