<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Filler_Battles">Filler Battles</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FAshura_Doji%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D24&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<ul><li>Ashura, <a href="/wiki/Kin%27emon" title="Kin&#39;emon">Kin'emon</a>, <a href="/wiki/Raizo" title="Raizo">Raizo</a>, <a href="/wiki/Kikunojo" title="Kikunojo">Kikunojo</a>, <a href="/wiki/Inuarashi" title="Inuarashi">Inuarashi</a> and <a href="/wiki/Shinobu" title="Shinobu">Shinobu</a> vs. <a href="/wiki/Queen" title="Queen">Queen</a></li>
<li>Ashura vs. <a href="/wiki/Holed%27em" title="Holed&#39;em">Holed'em</a></li></ul>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Anime_and_Manga_Differences">Anime and Manga Differences</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FAshura_Doji%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D25&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<p>In the manga, Ashura and his band of thieves only caught one of Holed'em's men setting fire to Mt. Atama. In the anime, Ashura and his group fight against Holed'em and his men, and Holed'em starts the fire while clashing with Ashura.<sup id="cite_ref-71" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-71">&#91;71&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Merchandise">Merchandise</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FAshura_Doji%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D26&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Video_Games">Video Games</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FAshura_Doji%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D27&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Playable_Appearances">Playable Appearances</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FAshura_Doji%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D28&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<ul><li><i><a href="/wiki/One_Piece_Bounty_Rush" title="One Piece Bounty Rush">One Piece Bounty Rush</a></i></li>
<li><i><a href="/wiki/One_Piece_Treasure_Cruise" title="One Piece Treasure Cruise">One Piece Treasure Cruise</a></i></li></ul>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Trivia">Trivia</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FAshura_Doji%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D29&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<ul><li>Like <a href="/wiki/Kurozumi_Tama" title="Kurozumi Tama">O-Tama</a>, he spoke in a dialect that is unique to a specific region of Japan. This area is known as <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Kagoshima_Prefecture" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Kagoshima Prefecture">Kagoshima</a>, one of the prefectures created during the <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Meiji_period" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Meiji period">Meiji period</a> as the country transitioned from the isolationism enforced by the Shogunate.</li>
<li>The names Shutenmaru and Ashura Doji are likely a reference to <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Shuten-d%C5%8Dji" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Shuten-dōji">Shuten-dōji</a>, a mythical oni leader from Japanese legends.</li>
<li>The middle kanji of his alias, "天"<span style="font-weight: normal"> (<span class="t_nihongo_kanji" lang="ja">ten</span><span class="t_nihongo_help"><sup><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Help:Japanese" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Help:Japanese"><span class="t_nihongo_icon" style="color:#00e;font:bold 80% sans-serif;text-decoration:none;padding:0 .1em;">?</span></a></sup></span>)</span>, is the Japanese kanji for "Heaven". This same kanji is seen on the sake bottle he carries.</li>
<li>Of every samurai present in Wano, Ashura Doji can be considered the closest to a typical ronin from Feudal Japan, being a samurai who fell into criminal life due to losing his master.</li></ul>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="SBS-Based_Trivia">SBS-Based Trivia</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FAshura_Doji%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D30&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<ul><li>The tree on top of Ashura’s head is modelled after the rakugo "Head Mountain".<sup id="cite_ref-72" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-72">&#91;72&#93;</a></sup></li>
<li>Ashura's favorite food is <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/mochi" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:mochi">mochi</a> kinchaku.<sup id="cite_ref-sbs96_10-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-sbs96-10">&#91;10&#93;</a></sup> Fittingly enough, mochi kinchaku is one of the main ingredients in <a href="/wiki/Foods#Oden" title="Foods">oden</a>, just as Ashura was one of <a href="/wiki/Kouzuki_Oden" title="Kouzuki Oden">Kouzuki Oden</a>'s main retainers.</li></ul>
